mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">崔永芬</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡彩影：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东佛山市张槎小学英语教师、法轮功学员。蔡彩影在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月迫害法轮功以来，她曾多次被绑架迫害，曾经被非法判刑七年，家庭破碎。蔡彩影<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被抓捕，被关押在佛山看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月左右，蔡彩影被佛山市禅城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，目前被关押在广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡恒军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省辛集市法轮功学员。河北辛集市南智邱镇东陈家庄村人，在深圳给儿子看孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日中午一点左右，深圳市龙田派出所闯入蔡恒军儿子家中，将蔡恒军抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在广东深圳庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。现关押于河北保定市监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡林华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员蔡林华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡伟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，哈尔滨市法轮功学员。大学本科毕业，从事财务统计工作多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日过遭抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，蔡伟华被入黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡玉嫦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省汕头市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，家住汕头市龙湖区外砂镇莲中村。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，原本幸福温馨的家，被中共迫害得支离破碎。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被金平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元；蔡玉嫦提起上诉；汕头市中级法院<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日枉法维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日左右，蔡玉嫦被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450658.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450658.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡予华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省三门峡市法轮功学员，女，二零二一年四月左右被判刑四年半，现已被劫持到河南省新乡女子监狱。蔡予华由于坚定修炼法轮功，在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年前被中共劳教（具体时间不详）。蔡予华由于在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向最高法院和检察院邮寄控告迫害元凶江泽民的控告信，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日晚上被抓捕、关押，家人被勒索财物，后又被判刑，在新乡女子监狱，受尽折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，蔡予华向有关部门邮寄了申诉控告信，要求返还并按时发放她在判刑期间被剥夺的养老保险金。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，蔡予华被三门峡陕州区警察从家中抓捕，关押在三门峡市看守所，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，后被送往新乡女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，长春市农安县法轮功学员，农民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨六点多钟，在农安县政府大楼对面，一群国保公安人员抓捕一家三口——蔡玉英、于娇茹母女，和这家老实巴交的男主人。那天，农安县非法抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。此次非法抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的，长春市政法委书记马延峰亲赴农安县部署非法抓捕行动，七月十三日，农安县政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”召开会议落实具体行动方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日判决书下到看守所：蔡玉英被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡智慧</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区法轮功学员，</span>蔡智慧在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被吉林警察抓捕到吉林省的看守所，后获悉其被吉林法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434767.html#211212222835-1"><b 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹爱兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，河南南阳油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年她修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，曹爱兰因为坚持信仰法轮大法，曾四次被绑架，两次判刑，累计陷冤狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局采取统一行动，在南阳地区开始绑架法轮功学员，两陷冤狱的法轮功学员曹爱兰老太被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曹爱兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹长起：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省临沂市蒙阴县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已年过七旬。其于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被抓捕、关押，后得知他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，已经被劫持到山东男子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/16/444998.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹春生：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，河南省郑州市高新区石佛办事处百炉屯村大街<span lang="EN-US">159</span>号居民，私营塑料制品生产经营业主，抗暴维权者、中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月以来，其房屋一直被郑州市高新区石佛办事处政府威胁强拆，部分财产已遭损坏，出于无奈，自此其走上拆迁维权之路；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其住房在被镇政府暴力强拆时家人竟被打伤；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其所开办工厂再次遭当地政府强拆；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，一批手持各种器械及大型机械的强拆者欲将其剩余房屋进行野蛮强拆，为保护家园，其全家奋起反抗，双方随发生激烈冲突，混乱中为了自卫，其将对方其中二人刺伤，最终导致一死一伤，自己也在冲突中受伤，之后逃走；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其被郑州警方在三门峡市灵宝县以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”拘捕，并关押于郑州市第三看守所；另有一名远房亲戚也因其在逃亡中曾在他家待过而被警方以涉嫌“窝藏罪”刑拘；据悉，其与强拆方发生冲突时，有村民远距离拍下一些照片和证据，后来不幸均被警方没收销毁；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案被郑州市中牟县检察院起诉至郑州市中牟县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，终被郑州市中牟县法院以“故意伤害罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。目前在河南省焦南监狱（河南焦作市映湖路焦南监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">454003</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，家住抚顺市顺城区永安桥北。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，七、八个便衣警察突然闯到她家中，抓捕了曹凤英，关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月传出她已被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前关押在抚顺市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/20/453354.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/20/453354.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹进兴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，唐山市农机局退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在中共当局的“敲门行动”中，他被唐山市路北区文化路派出所警察绑架。警察非法抄家持续了三个小时，家中大量私人物品被抢劫。在警察绑架过程中，曹进兴被摔伤，缝了几针。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕，在唐山市第一看守所被关押一年多，后背生了很多皮疹。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，河北唐山市路北区一审判处曹进兴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹培植：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，河南省义马市人，六四亲历者，《零八宪章》第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>批签署人，原“温馨小屋”群主，社会时政关注者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因参与年天安门民主运动并亲历“六四惨案”，遂自此改变了人生轨迹，坚定的走上一条中国民主运动不归路；曾因以民主推手、民权精英、博客骑士自许，而创建“温馨小屋”博客群，并在其努力经营下，使该博客群的点击量高达<span lang="EN-US">70</span>万人次；也正是因其频发民主信息和对中共当局不利的时政批评性信息，故而引起河南省当局的极度不悦与伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因其在微信群里传播“未经官方证实的海外消息，并对党和国家领导人有侮辱性言论”，遂被河南省义马市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又被义马市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；被押至今，一直无律师介入，家属急盼介入。目前被羁押于河南省渑池县看守所（河南省三门峡市渑池县英豪镇英东村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">472434</span>）。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_27.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_27.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曹三强</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：祖籍湖南，曾在当地创立家庭教会，是“中国福音会”牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年汶川地震后，曾从事四川基督教爱心工作，帮助学生及地震灾民度过难关。多年前，曹三强到云南普洱从事宣教、慈善救济及兴教办学事业，并在当地创办多所学校，帮助贫困儿童入学。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，他与基督徒景如霞从缅甸佤邦（缅甸第二特区）返国时，出于便利使用了非正式方式入境中国，被边防武警拦截拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日即被当地检察院以涉嫌“偷越国境罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日该案移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日该案在孟连县法院开庭，曹三强的亲友参加了旁听。尽管曹三强的辩护人刘培福律师认为，其当事人的行为不应构成犯罪，但他仍于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被云南省孟连县法院以“偷越国境罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元人民币，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。另一位基督徒景如霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，已当庭释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的曹三强牧师已转到位于云南省昆明市东郊王大桥的昆明监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">曹生祥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">青海西宁市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年六十六岁，本是西宁交通医院后勤科科长。因修炼法轮功，曾遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被西宁城北区公安抓捕，再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，目前被关押在门源监狱（海北州浩门监狱）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/22/%E9%9D%92%E6%B5%B7%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%B9%E7%94%9F%E7%A5%A5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-440336.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/22/%E9%9D%92%E6%B5%B7%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%B9%E7%94%9F%E7%A5%A5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-440336.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹艳芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，五十多岁，吉林省榆树市法轮功学员。曹艳芬<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被吉林市船营区公安分局欢喜岭派出所警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年后，已被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">柴惠芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江省宁波市余姚市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年生，河南郑州人，现定居在浙江省余姚市，经营一家电子公司。柴惠芹<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她从台湾看完神韵演出回宁波，在机场门口被抓捕，被关押在余姚看守所。她在台湾购买的两本《转法轮》和花钱买回的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>张神韵门票遭抢劫。柴惠芹被关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月后，以“取保候审”的形式回到家中后，被判缓刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再次被抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，她于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被关押带浙江女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/6/447312.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/6/447312.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹永亮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，县人，山西省汾西县永安镇郭村村民，职业不详，维权人士，中国在押维权人士。曾因汾西县政府在炸无证黑煤窑时，将住宅房屋震塌，且无人赔偿，自此走上维权上访之路，期间曾多次遭遇拘留，其户口本亦因累次上访而被警方恶意没收；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因在京上访时遭截访、欺骗和毒打等迫害，地方当局先是答应给其赔偿<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元，并当场支付现金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，打欠条<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，但将其带到北京市长安西街派出所后，即遭警方毒和搜身，致其后来长期身体虚弱、吐血不止、大小便流血，其刚拿到的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元赔偿金亦被抢走、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元欠条被撕毁，随后被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因继续上访又被右安门派出所警方毒打，并被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；此后，再次因上访而被拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，且每次都是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，当其在北京打工之时，被前来的汾西县警方突然抓回老家，遭毒打后被关至临汾市尧都区吴村看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，即被汾西县警方以“伪造居民身份证、寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被汾西县检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被山西省汾西县法院以“伪造身份证罪、寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；据悉，看守所关押期间，屡受非人折磨，曾被毒打导致其头破血流，眼睛看不见，眉骨骨折；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刑满获释；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，山西省汾西县当局因惧怕其在“百年党庆”时期再到北京上访，影响党国形象，随指派当地警方为其提供生活困难补助<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，以令其立刻中止去京上访；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其认为中共“百年党庆”敏感期已过，遂就到国家信访局继续提交申诉材料，岂料<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在北京暂住地遭遇截访；遣回原籍之后，先是送山西省蒲县看守所被拒收，又于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被送乡宁县隔离，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个多月后，在其家人委托的律师努力打听下终于获知，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>日，其案被山西省汾西县法院庭审宣判，最终被以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前被羁押于山西省临汾市尧都区看守所<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常珈瑄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，山西省临汾市人，退役军人，临汾市尧都区解放西路<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号“常家大院”（祖宅）继承人之一，著名维权公民，维权致残者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年以来，因其从清代传承下来的祖宅曾被山西省晋南专区地方国营建筑工程队借走，历经数十载后，借方竟不想再谈归还之事，其父常耀文遂被迫携其全家人走上投诉维权之路<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年，其父带着妻儿数十人举家欲迁回祖宅居住，租房方不仅不如约归还，反以昔日领导“现在都管不了”为由久拖不给，其父无奈，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，随一纸诉状将临汾市建筑工程总公司告上地方法院；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，临汾市人民法院派人向当年的证人、中保等数人取证，经过比对，认为证词皆与常耀文所诉情况一致，所以于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，法院对其案双方进行了调解；不料被告方一边应诉，一边却仍与中国建行银行临汾市支行办理房屋交割手续，临汾市法院针此最终判定：“买卖无效，撤销其违法买卖涉及本案房产的有关手续”；被告方（又即借房方）不服，提起上诉，后经临汾市中级法院二审裁决：支持一审裁判；但借房方仍不服判决，反复几次提起上诉，而当地的政府土地部门亦对此事久拖<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不予裁定 ；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，因临汾市建筑工程总公司谎称“上世纪<span lang="EN-US">50</span>年代已购得<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号院，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年被常耀文占用并在此院内违法建筑，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年临汾市国土资源局确权该院国有土地使用权归属该公司”，并以此为由将其父枉法诬告上法庭，要求其父“停止侵权、恢复原状、返还财产”；此案件被受理后，尧都区法院一审以“原告起诉状中涉及的违法建筑应当由有关行政执法部门查处，不属于法院民事受案范围”，驳回了该借房公司的起诉；该公司仍然不服，再次上诉，又经临汾市中级法院终审裁定：一审的裁定驳回起诉正确；但遗憾的是，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其父常耀文未等来土地证即与世长辞。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其母再度委托律师、其及其姊常春枝，提出土地权属申请；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，临汾市国土资源局受理了该案件，但此后除<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次发出延期调查处理通知书之外，一直未予办结；其全家在维权诉讼过程中，曾屡遭殴打侮辱，导致其父受伤卧床不起，其被临汾市规划局打断四根肋骨，成了残疾人；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其姐弟二人相继被临汾市警方抓捕，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”、 “妨碍公务罪”指定居所监视居住；后被正式逮捕被羁押于临汾市尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，常珈瑄因抗强拆，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在山西晋城监狱二监区服刑。何时开庭何时宣判，一概不知。同时被捕的其姐常春枝怎样，目前情况不详。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玮平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西人权律师，原陕西立刚律师事务所律师。常玮平律师因为代理所谓敏感案件，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被停业</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月，及后原本的执业律师事务所被注销，需要在半年内转到其他律师楼继续执业，否则执照会被吊销。后他异地转所至浙江，也受到阻碍。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日常玮平律师到杭州市西湖区法院递交诉状，起诉浙江省司法厅不履行调转律师档案法定职责。常律师自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日向浙江省司法厅提交了转入浙江左契律师事务所的申请后，该厅迄今未办理。常玮平律师被迫处于被吊销律师执业证书的状态。常玮平律师因厦门公民聚会案于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日晚在西安住处被西安公安局高新区分局带走，办案单位是宝鸡市公安局高新区分，后常玮平的妻子接到宝鸡高新分局国保大队电话，被告知常玮平因危害国家安全，已经被指定居所监视居住。随后其律师执业证遭注销。后于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">21</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日取保获释回家。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月后，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日常玮平又遭指定居所监视居住。常玮平被再次抓捕的原因是他在海外网站上发布视频控诉其遭受的令人发指的酷刑，遭宝鸡警方挟私报复。后律师申请对其取保，遭宝鸡警方拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日）家属收到了常玮平的逮捕通知书，他已被关到了秦岭山中的凤县看守所。著名人权律师常玮平案将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下在陕西省凤县法院不公开审理。此案已历时两年多月了，当局仍然不敢公开审理。后常玮平案经最高法院批准再被延期审理<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/2022726.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/2022726.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男、<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，曾用名常玉光，陕西省西安市人，西安市高陵区泾渭上城小区<span lang="EN-US">41</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">1</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">3</span>层<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号公民，基督徒，陕西光义爱圣印务公司法人代表，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起，因其所属印务公司大量印刷了与基督教信仰有关的数据及图书，随引起地方当局的高度关注与警惕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，西安市文化执法部门联合西安市国家安全部门对其公司进行了查封与鉴定，现场扣押各种宗教类书籍<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万余册，后又经陕西省新闻出版和电影质量检测中心对其中《改革宗信仰》等<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书鉴定，认定该<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书为“未经批准擅自印刷的出版物”的非法出版物，随于次日（<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），立刻与其妻李琛慧被西安市高陵区警方一并抓走，后被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被更换罪名以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被西安市高陵区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其在无印刷许可证的情况下经营印刷业务，印刷非法出版物，扰乱市场秩序，起行为均构成非法经营罪，故而应予以逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被西安市高陵区法院一审以“非法经营罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，经陕西省西安市中级法院二审裁决，最终仍然驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。目前仍被羁押于西安市高陵区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑，暂不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈柏清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省竹山县田家坝镇访民任治孝的代理人，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁的任治孝没有成家是孤身一人，从<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始就清水电站移民的补偿安置权益，不服地方法院的枉法裁判而进京上访，遭到地方政府、公安派出所无数次的截访，及非法拘禁黑监狱。后来，认识了竹山县双台乡鱼塘村的陈柏清，就委托陈柏清代理撰写举报控告材料。因其在潘口水电站移民时的安置补偿权益遭到损害而上访，在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初到省会武汉市举报控告镇、村官吏的违法行为，被押回当地竹山县上庸镇福利院黑监狱。陈柏清<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”拘留、抄家。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_3.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_3.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈大栗：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1994</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，本名陈思冶，北京市与广州市交替居住者，影像工作者和音乐爱好者，动物权利保护者，异见表达者，中国在押政治犯。自称具有“深度对话体质”，曾因为保护动物权利而吃素几年，后因身体健康原因被迫放弃；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，因去广州市越秀区海珠广场与现场无数人一起表达了对政府采取“动态清零”政策过度防疫的愤怒，遂立遭广州当局打压和秋后算账；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被广州市越秀区北京路派出所警方传唤带走，自此失联；后其家人得知，他被以“寻衅滋事”罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天；但至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其在办理了释放手续之后，又被突然截留转移，遂再度至今下落不明；针此，网友疑指其极可能已被越秀区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；据悉，因陈大栗身体属极度敏感性体质，本年度刚过<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次手术，尚处于漫长的康复过程中，故其家人及网友对当下信息不明的执法程序中，他能否得到基本的人权保障与合理健康的医疗、温饱条件等十分担忧。目前疑似被羁押于广州市越秀区看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_96.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_96.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈迪才：</span></b><a name="_Hlk54957732"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54957732;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，大学文化，户籍所在地是黄石市下辖阳新县黄颡口镇。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚，他的姐姐被她丈夫李生水家暴殴打，外甥女打电话给舅舅陈迪才打电话，随后陈迪才骑车到姐家，看见姐姐被打得躺在床上，地上有被扯下的几缕头发。陈迪才与姐夫李生水理论，李生水打电话举报陈迪才炼法轮功。晚十一点左右，黄石市黄石港区红旗桥派出所警察把陈迪才和她姐一家带到派出所，在陈迪才身上搜出几张真相币和含有法轮功内容的<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，派出所立即联系了黄石港区国保大队。陈迪才被关押、构陷一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被视频开庭，以捏造的「事实」判处陈迪才<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈法庆</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">浙江环保人士。<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，农民企业家出身。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年前，他曾经和江苏省环保人士吴立红自费在“纽约时报”刊登中英文环保公益广告，敦促当时刚上任的政治局常委，兑现环保承诺。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，陈法庆被当局以“组织领导传销活动”为由，刑事拘留。家属认为，该事件与中共十九大即将召开有关。家属称，陈法庆多年来不断受到当局打压，谋生遇到很多障碍。不到<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月前，他曾向习近平寄送锦旗，要求他及各级领导善待残疾人。后案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈庚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建省福州市平潭县法轮功学员，教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日早上，陈庚打算去学校给学生上课时，被围堵的警方抓捕，遭法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。陈庚据理上诉，却被驳回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，陈庚在被拘留<span lang="EN-US">275</span>天后，被劫入福清镜洋监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈公安：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省九江市人，九江市武宁县人，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因与所当地多名民主维权公民经常聚集聊天议事，并积极在微信群里发时政性贴文及视频讯息，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，遂与王林安、李玉荣和柯有斌等另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名民主维权好友分别被九江地区国保警方传唤带走，次日均被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其案被九江市武宁县警方提交到当地武宁县检察院，被检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕；截至当前，其被抓之后的各种具体信息均称不详，亦不知有否律师介入；与其熟识的网友指称，其被逮捕，应与中共二十大召开之际其等网络言论令当局不安有关，故而因言获罪。目前被羁押于九江市武宁县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_6.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈国江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年出生，贵州省籍人，化名陈天河、熊焰，又被外卖骑手与工运支持者称为陈生，早期曾作街边摆摊个体户和工地搬运工，前北京市某饭店餐厅老板，全国著名外卖平台“美团”和“饿了么”北京市快递员，“外送江湖骑士联盟” 微信群组建者，北京外卖骑士联盟“盟主”，外卖联盟维权者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自幼出生于贵州省一个农村家庭，在父母频繁争吵中度过童年；五年级时，曾因家贫而辍学，随后靠在街边摆摊、在工地搬砖度日；后又辗转来到北京，自此成为一名北漂；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾受雇于一家餐厅专职送餐；后又开始制作网页版订餐网站，承包了附近所有网吧的订餐业务，并用积累下来的积蓄开办了一家小型餐馆；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，又开办另一家较大型饭店，但因长期经营亏损，随被迫转而成为送外卖小哥，亦因此事，其妻与其离婚，携幼子另嫁；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年起，曾因在送外卖工作中发现骑手们的生存环境十分恶劣，送餐服务的单价不断下降，无休息日，事故频发却得不到保障，无话语权，遂与骑手朋友组建“外送江湖骑士联盟”微信群，其为“盟主”；在此期间，曾因经常慷慨解囊协助失意投靠人度过难关，且致力于帮助骑手同行维权和鼓励彼此互助，故而深受众人好评和敬意；曾录制过百余条视频，向社会讲述外卖骑手们的遭遇和心酸，希望赢得支持和关注；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因外卖平台统一压低骑手送餐单价，为维护外卖骑手权益，其力挺发动骑手们拒绝接单，称前<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天不送“美团”，后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天不送“饿了么”，并让其各自打印通知，贴在外卖箱后边；然而传单尚未发出，其旋即被北京警方抓走，共计拘留<span lang="EN-US">26</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，北京外卖快递员为了生计和响应疫情防控就地过年，继续留京工作跑单，但因“饿了么”、“美团”等外卖平台刻意设置额外超级工作量，以使快递员因完不成任务而被克扣奖金，其为追诉公道，再次组织同行抵制外卖平台压榨骑手的劳工权益，但很快遭打压，与多名相关快递员被北京市朝阳区警方抓捕，罪由不清，至今不予释放；外界普遍疑称，因其组建的“外送江湖骑士联盟”群组，已联系有上万名骑手，影响力甚大，成为实质上的外卖骑手“工会”和维权组织，遂令中共当局感到恐惧，故而被抓。陈国江的家属于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日收到了其被正式逮捕的通知书。目前被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所（北京市朝阳区朝阳北路<span lang="EN-US">29</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">100023</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东法轮功学员。广东雷州市白沙镇梛楠村人，后在湛江霞山区租住，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月末，在雷州市向民众发放法轮功资料的时候，被告，遭关押了几天后，获释，回到自己租住的房子。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初，陈海霞又被警察绑架、抄家。后遭判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在血压高不适合关押的情况下，中院维持冤判，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被关押到广州女子监狱迫害。目前，陈海霞被洗脑灌输、野蛮灌食，眼睛赤红、非常憔悴，仅一个月余，其境况令家人十分担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈皓恒：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，“雨伞运动”参与者，香港政党“社会民主连线”（简称“社民连线”或“社民连”）成员，前立法会议员助理，原“民间人权阵线（民阵）”召集人，民主派政治人士，中国在押政治犯。自小生长于香港，并从初中开始，因接触、了解到“六四”的历史而对社会政治产生浓厚兴趣，曾先加入中学生组织多次参与政治活动；中学毕业后，虽一度攻读旅游专业，但自从<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年参与“雨伞运动”之后决定辍学全程投入社会运动，故而自此加入香港民主政党“社民连”，并参与其他民主派组织，曾做过立法会议员助理，协助其参与竞选工作；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，曾因前民阵召集人岑子杰被香港国安局警方关押，迫于形势需要新人补位，其随接手民阵召集人一职；又因该组织原是结合香港众多民主派政党及公民团体的平台，但自其担任召集人之后，有消息盛传民阵可能卷入一场《国安法》案件，随民主党、公民党等香港主流政党被迫先后宣布退出，致使民阵变得更为孤军作战；后又因其多次参与“反送中”游行示威，让其累积不少筹办大型活动的经验，包括如何向警方申请游行、怎样联络媒体、怎样摆放街站、撰写和发布声明等等，故而数月以来，民阵的中坚力量虽只剩下其一个人，但依然把工作做到很好；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因“港区国安法”的出台和实施促使香港爆发了大规模的“反送中”示威抗议活动，反对北京缩减香港自由的示威民众情绪激昂；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其深度参加了民主派港人的国庆节大游行和反送中抗议行动，被港警拘捕，被控涉嫌涉嫌“组织未经批准集结罪”和“煽惑他人参与未经批准集结罪”等共计<span lang="EN-US">14</span>项罪名；后经几次香港区域法院提堂庭审，先被获刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，且已入监服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被香港东区法院再行审判，被指控因参与<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年在港岛区的非法集结，被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，鉴于其承认该控罪，最终法官判处其在原有刑期上加刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月，共被判囚<span lang="EN-US">22</span>个月。目前疑似在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈恒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">福州法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被连江县城关派出所警察抓捕，被转到罗源县隔离十几天后，再被转关到连江县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，他被逮捕。长乐检察院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日将他起诉到长乐法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陈恒收到长乐法院对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈洪伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，别名陈宏伟，辽宁省康平县人，康平县体校家属楼北栋<span lang="EN-US">5</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">501</span>号公民，辽宁伟业律师事务所律师，贪腐举报人，维权律师，中国在押维权人士。自成为执业律师并在辽宁伟业律师事务所任职以来，一直勤勉工作，认真执业；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾因康平县开发区管委会与开发区朝阳工业园内养殖小区的被拆迁户谈判陷入僵局，被该管委会聘请为法务工作代理，前去与被拆迁户协商拆迁事宜；为支持政府工作，其接受了此一聘请委托，并以先难后易等方式耐心做到与拆迁户的协商工作；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾先后三次从开发区财政局借款共计<span lang="EN-US">103</span>万元，且自搭<span lang="EN-US">1.46</span>万元，全部如数如约支付给被拆迁户作为补偿款，得到众被拆迁户的广泛认可；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因对当地政府的招标行为及相关部门官员的贪腐问题不满，声称要对县里的主要领导温某予以举报，随后不久立遭打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区警方以涉嫌“行贿罪”抓捕，后被留置；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被以涉嫌“贪污罪、行贿罪”转为刑拘，后知被疑指与十几年前其协助当地开发区拆迁和送某领导洗浴卡有关；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市和平区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并被关押于沈阳市和平区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区法院一审以“贪污罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；以“行贿罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；以“诈骗罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万元，数罪并罚决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元；其不服判决，立即上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，经沈阳市中级法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判；其坚称无罪，再次提起申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，经沈阳市中级法院再审，依然维持原判，驳回申诉；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。目前仍被羁押于沈阳市和平区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑尚不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈鸿元</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：男，广东揭阳法轮功学员。家住揭阳市榕城区东兴街道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被榕城区国保、榕东派出所警察抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日他被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，他被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金八万元。陈鸿元不服，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，揭阳市中级法院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，陈鸿元被关押到广东省四会监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈华良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男广东省惠州市博罗县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，贵州省贵阳市人，家住贵阳市云岩区狮子路。他<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年毕业于浙江省金华供销学校并留校任教，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年调任贵州商学院任教师。因坚持修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被开除公职。陈华良在灵泉学堂教国学。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>时左右，博罗县公安局国保大队几乎倾巢出动，和九潭派出所警察一块，以查经营为由，从邻居家闯入灵泉学堂，查抄。查抄中，发现有法轮功书籍，警察将赵天华抓捕，他的妻子蔡惠斌、灵泉学堂的教师陈华良、练日光一起被抓捕，被关押到博罗县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被惠州市惠城区法院判决：陈华良被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陈开奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">41</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省莆田市人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被福建省宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，其与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨雄、庄友布、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，陈开奇被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈继海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住吉林市丰满区二道乡张家村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吉林市公安局及下属派出所警察抓捕至少有<span lang="EN-US">21</span>名法轮功学员、二名家属，法轮功学员陈继海、宋德满是其中两位。被关押一年余，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈继海和宋德满分别被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现在吉林省第二监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈家鸿：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，广西壮族自治区北流县隆盛镇平坡村人，又名陈文胆，字数真，早年为广西北流县鸭壤小学教师，知名业余书法家、字画家，原南宁市百举鸣律师事务所执业律师，敏感案件代理人，中国人权律师团成员，人权律师，政治犯。自从成为“百举鸣律师事务所”（现已被当局取缔）中一名执业律师以来，因长期参与维权敏感案件，追求民主人权并为之积极发声，随屡遭中共当局严打逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因积极介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，而遭广西警方的持枪围困；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因同一事件，其介入维权行为被广西律师协会视为违规，从而被该律师协会给予“公开谴责行业处分的通报”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其被北流县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕、刑拘，其家被查抄；之后，其又被北流县检察院以同罪由予以批捕，并被指控因其反对官员腐败、呼吁建立民主宪政等带有政治倾向的公开言论、书法作品及行为艺术等涉及挑战现政权，尤其是其中一副书法作品，内含“成立暗杀突击队！清算邪恶官僚，加速民主进程”等激进敏感字眼，触犯了政府的相关法律条例，其行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案件被地方检察院移交至玉林巿中级法院起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，终被玉林市中级法院在其辩护律师未到场的情况下，一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；此前被羁押于广西玉林市看守所。陈家鸿<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被传唤，后又被刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名“寻衅滋事”，办案机关是广西北流市治安大队。家人噤声，目前尚无律师介入。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/34.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/34.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈建芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海著名维权人士、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“曹顺利人权捍卫者纪念奖”获奖人。陈建芳从一位抗争土地权的农民开始，长期从事维权活动。十多年前，她家的土地被上海市政府和房屋开发商非法征收和抢占，因得不到合法合理的安置补偿，走上了上访之路捍卫自己的权益。在多年的维权与打压的磨练中，陈建芳逐渐成为当地土地征收和房屋拆迁受害者的代言人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈建芳和曹顺利女士共同接受邀请，参加当月在日内瓦举办的人权培训活动并同时观摩联合国人权理事会会议。陈建芳在广州机场被阻拦出境。在同一天，曹顺利女士在北京机场被警方拦截并被强迫失踪。警方将陈建芳带回上海并对其拘留、调查讯问、并密切监视多日。陈建芳的人权倡导活动，招来当局对她不断地打击报复，包括恐吓，殴打和任意拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早晨八点陈建芳在家中遭上海警方秘密抓捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，被上海市浦东新区检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”批捕，被指控因为聚集举牌、拉横幅、网络言论等违法了国家法律。后遭起诉。遭中共当局司法机关的违法阻扰，律师一直无法介入案件。目前陈建芳女士被羁押于上海市看守所。当局始终不准其代理律师会见。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">后</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日获悉陈建芳女士遭中共当局构陷“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46-20231021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46-20231021.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈剑雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈进新，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年出生，湖北省赤壁市人，网名陈剑雄，“赤壁五君子”之一，南方街头运动践行者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年以来，曾多次参与国内的围观声援活动，勇于多次举牌、拉横幅表达对民主宪政的政治要求，是南方街头运动杰出代表之一，亦因此曾多次遭到中共警方的拘留、刑拘、酷刑和强行驱赶等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因与袁小华、袁奉初、黄文勋等民主维权者在湖北省赤壁市宣传民主政治，而被当地警方以“煽动颠覆国家政权”为由刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾与民主维权者谢文飞在广东省佛山市街头举横幅，要求“废除一党专制，建立民主中国”，而被佛山警方再次以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，并关押在天河区看守所，备受酷刑折磨，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因参加山东曲阜薛福顺非正常死亡事件观察团奔赴曲阜追查真相，多次在曲阜遭警方欧打和驱赶；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因到黑龙江省声援“建三江律师被拘事件”，而被当警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因到武汉市与多名友人会见佛教法师徐志强，被武汉警方抓走，又被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因再次前往河南郑州参与公民声援“郑州十君子事件”，并到河南焦作市声援“张小玉夫妇杀警事件”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方在郑州第三看守所附近抓走，且被湖北省赤壁市警方直接报检察院以涉嫌“扰乱社会公共秩序罪”执行逮捕，羁押于赤壁市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被湖北省咸宁市赤壁市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，刑满释放；出狱后，其追求民主意志弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因与维权友人袁兵、梁一鸣去赤壁市公安局国保大队投诉出狱后遭长期监控、骚扰等事宜，终因双方理念不同、争论颇激而不欢而散；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被赤壁市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被赤壁市检察院正式批捕，并被羁押于赤壁看守所：<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，终被湖北省赤壁市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经咸宁市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刑满释放。此前在湖北省咸宁监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，陈剑雄又被警方抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日代理律师马纲权律师在湖北通城县检察院视频会见了被羁押的湖陈剑雄，获悉目前案件已移送湖北通城县检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_45.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_17.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_17.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人毕业于清华大学法学院，中国资深的媒体人，先后在《南方周末》、《中国青年报》、《新京报》、《人民日报》等媒体上发表了<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多篇评论文章。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年以中国青年报记者身份踢爆武汉女大学生卖淫现象，造成轰动，但却被解雇；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年作为公益时报主编，签发批评文章，触怒当局再被炒；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月因“批评政府过多”遭人民日报解除人民网江苏视窗执行总编职务。陈杰人多年来发表数千文章，希望推进新闻自由，并倡导以网络为平台的草根监督和公民表达。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span
