lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在发放法轮功资料时，遭八里湾镇派出所警察抓捕、关押。近日得知，程连连已被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，张桂英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。更多详情待查。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442538.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程学珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。程学珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程渊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，广东省深圳市常驻居民，中国民间公益机构“长沙富能”创办人（之一）、工作人员，乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者等群体维权诉讼代理人，中国在押政治犯。因从事公益维权活动<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余年，曾代理过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多起乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者维权诉讼案，颇受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾首例成功代理江西省进贤县艾滋就业歧视案，为当事人争得赔偿，经多家媒体报导而广为人知，但亦引起中共当局的高度警觉及跟踪监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，突然被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从深圳跨境带走，并被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；审讯期间，被多次问及其在长沙富能所做的工作内容、资金来源及其近期外出活动（含去香港，与香港记者录像等）都做些什么等细节详情；据悉，被抓当天，其家属多受牵连，其妻竟被戴黑头套遭无辜审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">17</span>小时，其<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁半幼女遭惊吓，夜晚睡觉出现抽搐和梦呓，白天表现惊恐异常，其兄程浩、其老父亲等均遭警告恐吓；其代理律师欲了解案件详情遭绝，仅告知其罪名及法定的拘留期限；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭起诉，并被遭强行委派官派律师，对家属严密封锁，拒不见面。家属外界都无法获知案情进展。已经开庭审理，家属仍然对信息一无所知。被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：长沙富能公益案之程渊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑，</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现在于湖南赤山监狱服刑。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程渊在赤山监狱被关禁闭三个月，强迫劳动暴瘦<span lang="EN-US">12</span>斤头发全白<span lang="EN-US">, </span>程渊家人收到家书伤心落泪<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/12.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/12.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程志春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省四平市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年生。程志春曾曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，程志春被四平市铁西区仁兴派出所抄家、抓捕，由于疫情暂放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日左右，程志春被公安方面下书告知，被四平铁西检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日后执行。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在吉林省女子监狱遭受迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%9C%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B3%E5%B8%8278%E5%B2%81%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E7%A8%8B%E5%BF%97%E6%98%A5%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-430476.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%9C%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B3%E5%B8%8278%E5%B2%81%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E7%A8%8B%E5%BF%97%E6%98%A5%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-430476.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">成梅花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省清远市连州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月生，女。中专毕业，家住清远市连州市。她<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，因讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，她多次遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，她被清远市公安局劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被连州公安局拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，成梅花在家中被连州警察抓捕，她的家被查抄，家里的法轮功书籍和资料被抄走。关押到连山拘留所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，她被英德市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447350.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447350.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次成加材（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，又名次成坚参，笔名“秀真”，前四川甘孜州白玉佛学院僧人，前西北民族大学中文文学专业学生，西藏知名青年藏汉双语作家，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年进入四川甘孜州白玉佛学院为僧，学习藏传佛教知识，截止<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾先后在色达五明佛学院及德格协庆寺等多个寺庙进行过深造，并在此期间勤耕不缀，于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年出版发行《雪域悲歌》、《雪域命运》等多部藏文著作；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年底还俗进入西北民族大学攻读中文文学写作专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年在该大学与其他同学联合创办了《新一代》藏文杂志，担任主编，同时，他还在藏人文化网开设的“秀真博客”里，用中文撰写过多篇文章，其中著名的有《丑陋的拉萨》、《那一夜》、《那些年、那些事》等等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因其多次在大学里举办各种被政府视为非法主题的讨论会，触及了当局的敏感神经，随被当局开除学籍，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月返乡后又开办了一所业余学校，向家乡青年进行免费藏汉双语教学。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，由于比如县比如乡莫阿村、孟庆村和达塘乡等地发生多处藏人示威行动，以抗议当局强行开展“爱国再教育、家家挂红旗”的政治宣讲活动，故而被警方指控在县学校学生集体抗议和民众绝食示威等事件中有“煽动分裂国家”、“破坏社会稳定”、“公开发表非法言论”之嫌，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被警方拘捕并抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被西藏自治区高级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”和“破坏社会稳定罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">次成嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州夏河县九甲乡人，夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。自幼即进入拉卜楞寺为僧；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因对中共当局高压严管制度的不满，甘肃省甘南州夏河县发生了大规模僧俗藏人的抗议游行，其亦参与其中；又因被当局视为带头抗议者，随在当局对抗议藏民展开大逮捕后被迫逃离；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被甘南州警方在舟曲县抓捕刑拘，并送至甘肃省安全厅看守所关押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其不服上诉，后经甘南州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；</b>据悉，其在关押期间，曾惨遭刑讯逼供；从被捕至判刑以来，其私聘律师权、亲属探视权及到法庭旁听审判权均被拒绝；因其行为仅为以和平抗议方式来表达内心诉求，却遭司法枉法重判，故而随后又在夏河县城、拉卜楞寺院内外出现大量抗议传单。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，次成嘉措获减刑，刑期减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又经甘肃省天水市中级法院批准，被二次减刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，其可能将于<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年刑满。目前疑似在甘肃省天水监狱（甘肃省天水市秦城区建设路<span lang="EN-US">196</span>号 ，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">741000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_27.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_27.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次旺（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">西藏索县赤多乡人，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，索县赤多乡珍达寺僧人，藏族良心犯。因关注西藏问题，被中共当局长期秘密监控，并被警方几次拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被当地警方第一次刑捕，非法关押半年后取保候审释放。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日第二次又被刑拘，当时和他一同遭捕的还有珍达寺诵经师仓央嘉措、僧人阿次和坚参。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年初左右，被中共西藏当局强行指控非法，以不知由罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次旺嘉措：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tsewang Gyatso</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，中国在押政治犯。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾， 随于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">仓央嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区那曲人，藏族僧人，那曲地区索县赤多乡珍达寺（又称直达寺）诵经师、财务主管，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共当局发现西藏那曲地区索县有人利用手机和微信传播所谓 “禁止材料”（如转发印有达赖喇嘛的图片、传播涉及民族尊严的歌曲及透露被封锁的地方消息等），且在围墙上喷涂“西藏独立”等字样，遂展开大规模抓捕行动；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，多名当地僧侣及村民被当局以莫须有罪名拘捕，多数人长期下落不明，仓央嘉措亦于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被当地警方从寺庙驻地抓走，后以涉嫌“与境外联系”及“煽动他人反政府”罪由刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被当局以“向外界保持联络”和“鼓励该寺年轻僧人反抗中国政府活动”等罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被羁押于西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丛霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，丛霞外出贴法轮功材料，被大连西岗区国保大队和西岗区八一路派出所抓捕。后丛霞被构陷到大连西岗区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上诉，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二审被维持冤判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，辽宁大连法轮功学员丛霞被从大连看守所转至沈阳女子监狱，因大连疫情原因，至今不许探视。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html</span></b></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">楚继东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（又名褚继东）<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原天津市大港油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，楚继东进京和平请愿，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；因他坚持信仰，再被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，再加期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，那就是<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，又连续被关押到天津多个劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年获悉，其在流落到宁夏后被抓捕，遭到残酷迫害，楚继东绝食抵制迫害至少有<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多天。据悉已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其他情况待查。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/3/442030.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/3/442030.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆维权人士。崔斌早在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因见义勇为，帮助消防武警官兵救人时，膝盖被武警踩伤，从而造成二级伤残。但重庆市政府不仅不依法承认他的见义勇为行为，更不按照相关法律政策给予奖励和救助，在万般无奈之下，他被迫走上了上访之路。期间，多次遭到重庆维稳部门删帖封号、监视居住、非法拘禁、拘留、殴打等一系列迫害。由此，崔斌由一位访民，逐渐成长为一名民主维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年因在北京二中院围观浦志强案而被抓进久敬庄，被关押五天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年参与声援郭飞雄签名活动，并在高笋塘步行街广场公开绝食以示声援，再遭传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月两会期间，崔斌因在北京拦截两会代表车辆，在重庆驻京办被关了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天黑监狱。之后被地方警察押送回家，再遭万州警方<span lang="EN-US">"</span>监视居住<span lang="EN-US">"</span>软禁一年。期间因外出没有事前“报告”，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。当地维稳部门一直是崔斌为“眼中钉肉中刺”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日崔斌就曾遭受过一次黑社会人员的殴打，那次是因为他进京上访，被重庆维稳部门所忌恨，于是他们指使黑社会人员用杀猪刀砍断了他双手的八根筋健和三根手指骨，并且全身多处被暴打砍伤。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，崔斌背着写有“孙政才独裁暴政腐化之风还在重庆漫延，重庆人民生活在水生火热之中”的牌子在高笋塘步行街广场游行，之后又穿着印有“当人民恐惧政府即为暴政”文化衫拍照并在网上传播，又遭传唤抄家。崔斌的处境日益艰难。长期以来，崔斌一直在当地警方的严密监控中，并被以各种方式，限制或变相限制其人身自由，尤其外出受到更明显的限制。崔斌自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日突然失联，后获悉：崔斌为自卫杀了维稳警察派去迫害他的黑帮人员，后遭刑事拘留。先是关押在重庆万州看守所。后获悉崔斌遭到起诉判刑，一直关押在重庆万州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，重庆维权公民前往万州看守所给崔斌上账<span lang="EN-US">,</span>遭到拒绝，后经询问得知崔斌已被判死缓，已由重庆万州看守所转到重庆蜀都监狱关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔桂芬<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市东营法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，东营市公安局、分局、市国保支队、区国保大队及六户派出所、胜利派出所、新区派出所实施了抓捕，当时共有包括王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡在内的十多名法轮功学员被抓捕、抄家。其中，王霞因身体原因，被“取保候审”，崔桂芬、王沐怡两人被关押于东营市看守所。山东省东营市东营区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡进行开庭宣判。法官闫晓辉在没有任何法律依据的情况下对她们作出了非法判决。王霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万五千元；崔桂芬被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款两万元；王沐怡被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">崔建秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东日照法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">日照市莒县小店镇薛家孟堰村人，崔建秀是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在夏庄镇给一位清洁工一份真相资料后，被夏庄镇中共党委干部岳青海恶意举报，被夏庄镇派出所不法警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月上旬，在北京律师做出有理有据的无罪辩护情况下，山东省日照市五莲县法院仍旧判崔建秀<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。崔建秀不服判决，已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/24/2022-3-24.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/24/2022-3-24.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔兰琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省任丘市吕公堡乡法轮功学员，吕公堡乡辛安庄村人。崔兰琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在北村讲真相，告诉人们瘟疫中如何自救，被吕公堡派出所巡警绑架。崔兰琴被关押在看守所，据悉于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日开庭。崔兰琴女儿在过年前给辩护律师打电话得知，她的妈妈被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔太：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950 </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名崔泰，圣名奥斯定（<span lang="EN-US">Agostino Cui Tai</span>），河北省张家口市人，天主教徒，河北省张家口市宣化教区主教，有“献祭的羔羊”之称，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年，曾在河北保定修道院培育后而晋铎（即类似于职位晋升），并由河北省易县教区师恩祥主教祝圣（即任命主教的一种仪式）为神父；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，又被梵蒂冈天主教教宗本笃十六世任命为河北省张家口市宣化教区的助理主教，协助主教赵克勋（<span lang="EN-US">Tommaso Zhao Kexun</span>）的神职工作；然而，正是基于其对国际正统天主教的认知和竭力在教会里牧养教友，虽被教会同工及教友们共认为是一位生活简朴，严于律己，充满圣德的好牧者，并被誉为“献祭的羔羊”，但却因不愿认同中共政权控制下的天主教爱国教会的权威性，随受打压和迫害；曾被当局多次非法拘押，并遭软禁和被强迫旅游累计长达<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年；拘押期间，曾因拒不说出有关宣化教区主教赵克勋的确切信息（含<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年赵去世后的埋葬地址）而惨遭酷刑；后因长期被羁押，河北省当局从<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起，准许其在中国农历新年及中秋节等重要节日，可获暂时假释回家数天，然而在复活节之前又会再被警方带走，或被要求送到指定的关押地点；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其因农历春节将至而被暂时获释回家，但时逢疫情大流行，其须与家人共处到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才能返回；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被张家口市宣化区警方突然再次抓捕刑拘，罪名不清；失联至今，一直不被释放；后获悉，其此次被抓皆因之前曾发布过三份文告，并公开自己是被罗马教廷承认的主教身份，但此主教身份却不被中共当局接受，故其公开主教身份的行为则被视为违法。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_2.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_2.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔永芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省衡水市景县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，退休职工。她的丈夫孟凡胜，六十岁，退伍军人，家住河北省衡水市景县。夫妇俩在北京帮助儿子看孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，孟凡胜和崔永芬夫妇在北京海淀区一小区内照看四岁的孙子，发放法轮功真相卡片，被人恶意举报，遭跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，崔永芬和孟凡胜在他们的儿子家被北京市海淀区公安分局和田村路派出所警察抓捕，被抄家，被关押到北京海淀看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，孟凡胜被释放，回到在北京的儿子家。崔永芬继续被关押在北京海淀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月崔永芬被北京海淀区山后法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金三千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/6/448758.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">董广平、董洪义</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董瑶琼、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">董怡然</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、董勇勇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董云仙</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜贺先、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜金花、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜景义</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜荣、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜振田、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜志俊</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段守珍、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段燕林</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、段宜法、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）、多杰扎才（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达吾提汗﹒达尔古色孜（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县人，哈萨克族，博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县牧民，人权捍卫者。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县先后有<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多哈萨克族人（不分年龄、职业，甚至有年轻学生及政府公务员等）因“在微信群里，讨论如何移民哈萨克斯坦国”事宜被中共当局抓捕，其亦因关注移民事宜，并积极协助哈萨克村民移民哈萨克斯坦而在此次当局大抓捕中遭受迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月突然被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全罪”传唤、刑拘，后很快被温泉县检察院正式批捕，被指“帮人移民到哈萨克斯坦”就是犯了严重的政治问题。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县法院一审以“危害国家安全罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。其不服，已提起上诉。据悉，羁押期间曾惨遭酷刑毒打，病危住院，但出院后仍被立即重判，其要求聘请辩护律师也被拒绝。目前被羁押于新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与赞查（藏）二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">代群英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省泸州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，纸箱厂退休职工，家住泸州市江阳区国窖社区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，代群英等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员到合江县自怀镇赶场时被抓捕，随后被批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员被合江法院判刑，其中代群英被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被关押到成都龙泉女子监狱四监区迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">代玉珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省曲靖市麒麟区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在讲法轮功时遭人举报，第二天她在家中被麒麟区国保大队警察抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬，曲靖市中级法院对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%9B%B2%E9%9D%96%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%BB%A3%E7%8E%89%E7%8F%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-445305.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%9B%B2%E9%9D%96%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%BB%A3%E7%8E%89%E7%8F%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-445305.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴启鸿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">牡丹江市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年被抓捕构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，关押在呼兰监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月传出他被呼兰监狱严重迫害，他在狱中坚持炼功，被打得胆囊粉碎，生命垂危。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/10/450612.html#22109233444-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/10/450612.html#22109233444-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴耀廷：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Benny Tai Yiu-ting</span>，香港人，基督徒，香港法律学者，前香港大学法律学院副院长和副教授，“占中三子”，民主派意见领袖，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长于香港；<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代，中学毕业后曾就读于香港大学法律系，获取法律学士学位后，又取得法律深造证书，并在英国伦敦大学获得法律硕士学位；早年曾有浓烈的“中国情怀”，喜读中文和中国历史，后在大学期间，因吸收民主自由思想而认识到一国之强大不只是富国强兵，而是让它走向宪政，遂研究兴趣转为宪法、宪政、公法、法律和政治及宗教的关系、人权及参与式民主等，并成为民主派意见领袖；大学毕业后，曾在民主派领袖李柱铭办公担任法案助理，并是《香港基本法咨询委员会》两位学生代表之一，同时对“一国两制”的实施提出了批判与质疑；之后曾多年在香港大学法律系当副教授、并曾在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2008</span>年期间担任法律学院副院长；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因提出“让爱与和平占领中环”观念而闻名，并认为香港若未能有“真正普选”，即应该参与占领行动以争取<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年香港行政长官选举得以有“真正选择”；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因先后提出雷动计划、风云计划及民主派<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选等行动，而赢得香港市民的极大支持和响应，但却屡遭亲共建制派人士及媒体攻击。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，随着港版国安法的正式实施，其很快被香港国安警方拘捕，被控曾因发起“占领中环”运动，并于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-28</span>日在香港中环金钟不同地点“煽惑他人”或“煽惑他人煽惑”非法阻碍行车道，因而被捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被西九龙裁判法院庭审裁决“串谋犯公众妨扰罪”和“煽惑他人犯公众妨扰罪”罪名成立；至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被判监<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个月；其不服判决，提起上诉，并申请保释；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，在服刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，终被获准以<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万港元保释等候上诉，并要交出旅游证件，不可离开香港；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-26</span>日其上诉在香港高级法院被聆讯；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其保释被撤回而返监；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其上诉最终被驳回；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，其副教授一职被香港大学校委会以在“占领中环”运动中有“不当行为”为由解聘，同期，其与另外二人又被廉政公署以在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年协调民主派初选时涉嫌选举开支非法行为等为罪由起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被香港区域法院又以“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”等罪名判囚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月；并与之前罪刑同期执行；截至目前，其等多人涉嫌民主派初选案，因系漫长而系列的审讯，故其仍需在押，继续候审。目前在香港大屿山石壁监狱服刑。</span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_69.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴之颖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，家住上海市普陀区新村路。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害后，因坚持信仰，她一直被中共当局监控、跟踪、上门骚扰等，被迫离家出走。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，她在山东被抓捕，后被劫持回上海，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，在上海松江女子监狱遭受迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，戴之颖被河南洛阳警方跨省抓捕，当日晚戴之颖被河南洛阳警方劫持离开上海，关押在河南洛阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，戴之颖被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。她家中有<span lang="EN-US">88</span>岁老母亲（也是法轮功学员），现在独居在家。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/2/445670.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/2/445670.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丹增曲培（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生，西藏自治区那曲市色尼区达前乡人，西藏知名企业家、慈善家，藏语言文化及生态环境保护者，藏人民生问题关切者，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国政治犯。近年来，作为一名杰出的藏族企业家，因常年致力于保护藏语言文化和生态环境，促进藏人的团结意识，以及将自己的收入捐给慈善事业等，故而深受各地藏人的称赞和尊重；但也正因如此，却被中共西藏当局视为需要极度关注和严控防范的异己对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，当其从四川省成都市出差返回西藏拉萨时，在拉萨贡嘎机场突遭拉萨警方围堵与拦截，并就其携带私人物品及其住宅进行搜查；后因发现其存有一些与政治有关的书籍和一副达赖喇嘛的法相，遂被强制带走，自此失踪；后知其在被单独拘押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多之久后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被西藏自治区拉萨市中级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”、“非法向境外发送情报罪”和“资助危害国家安全活动罪”等多罪枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并没收所有个人财产；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，经西藏自治区高级法二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前在拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓成开：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">绵阳市三台县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，绵阳市法轮功学员柳涛与三台县法轮功学员邓成开到三台县芦溪镇去买东西被抓捕。柳涛被关押在绵阳市看守所，邓成开被关押在三台县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，柳涛、邓承开被绵阳市三台县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金二千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州市法轮功学员。曾兴阳妻子，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖南省衡阳市人，大学毕业，在培训机构任职。曾兴阳、妻子邓芳、妹妹曾跃玲，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被天河区公安分局国保和石牌派出所警察抓捕，关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海珠区法院对<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人判刑，曾兴阳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邓芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；曾跃玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。邓芳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓光英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆访民，被强制关押精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">23</span>点邓光英在北京市丰台区吕村被朱家坟派出所抓捕至今，邓光英的家人至今没有收到任何拘押通知。邓光英父亲还透露，地方政府的官员曾多次上门，要求在邓光英属于精神病人的材料上签字。对地方政府的无理要求，邓光英的父亲予以断然拒绝。一个没有任何精神病症状的正常人，只不过因为信访反映问题与争取自身权益，表达诉求，就属于精神病人，就要拘禁于精神病院，这就是社会主义官僚的固有思维，然而用践踏国家法律与公民人权的方式。至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月仍被精神病，未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓国行</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河南商水县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，河南商水县姚集乡白茬村人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬去街上买馍时跟民众讲法轮功，遭人恶告，被警察抓捕到商水拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后被劫持到商水看守所关押。当时邓国行拒绝所谓“转化”，警察说：不转化永远不让出去。邓国行绝食反迫害，要求无条件放人。警察又利用灌食方式迫害邓国行。邓国行被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押在郑州新密监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓洪成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，湖南省岳阳市人，网名“成主民”，微博名“湘人血性”，自由职业者，广东省深圳市龙岗区阪田街杨美东四巷<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号租住户，深圳同城聚会公民，民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因邓洪成与肖兵、王威、李南海等多人在深圳市五和餐厅聚餐，席间李南海与肖兵被陌生人拍照（事后得知是国保），<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日中午，深圳市警方前往餐厅调查，手拿李南海、肖兵的照片要求工作人员指认，当天午后邓洪成与深圳维权公民肖兵、沈力、李南海、王威被警方扣押，自此失联；其侄子邓剑峰与同城聚餐公民丁岩、董凌鹏、王军及等得知消息之后前往其住处（深圳市杨美村五巷）寻找，亦遭失联；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其在江西的家属被当地派出所警察查问，且拒绝透露当邓洪成下落及具体情况；后获知，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其叔侄二人被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住，其侄子邓剑锋后被取保候审释放；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，邓洪成被深圳市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓棨然：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1989</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，香港湾仔骆克道金乐大厦某公司售货员，香港反对逃犯条例修订草案运动（简称反修例运动）参与者，中共眼中的“港独”分子，民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因参加香港反修例运动，而香港岛湾仔区警方在在其所供职的湾仔骆克道金乐大厦一单位内被搜出汽油弹原材料，遂被拘捕并被控“串谋意图纵火、管有任何物品意图摧毁或损坏财产罪”；后虽被法院获交保释放，但其后由于未出席法庭聆讯，遂被法庭发布通缉令，同时没收其保释金；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，又因不满中共当局在香港实施港版“国安法”（全称“中华人民共和国香港特别行政区维护国家安全法”），故而与香港友人、民主派人士乔映瑜联合组织多人从香港偷渡到台湾，并由其负责购买偷渡船只、参加培训学习基本驾驶快艇技能、购买偷渡所需食物及物品等；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人分别与具有共同理念和追求的香港公民郑子豪、张铭裕、张俊富、严文谦、黄伟然、李子贤、李宇轩、郭子麟等共计<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人联系，相约次日凌晨统一在香港西贡布袋澳码头会合，然后驾舟一同偷逃香港，前往台湾；但不幸的是，其等行踪很快被早有预料、监控的广东省管辖海域的深圳海警局查获，其等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>港人随即被深圳市盐田区警方以涉嫌“偷越国境罪”等刑拘，并被送深圳盐田看守所关押；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">12</span>港人被深圳市盐田区检察院正式批捕，其中，其被指控因与乔映瑜一同“根据他人安排，策划组织多人从香港偷渡至台湾”，以“企图把香港从中国分裂出去”，故而此行为已与香港《国安法》之相关规定相抵触；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案被深圳市盐田区警方提交盐田区检察院审查起诉，至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其中涉案<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被检察院提起公诉（另<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人因属未成年人，故被检察院以“自愿认罪认罚”而决定不予起诉）；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人案在深圳市盐田区法院被公开庭审，并被当庭宣判；其中，其被以“组织他人偷越边境罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日；与其同案的乔映瑜亦被以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，其余<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人均被以“偷越边境罪”统一判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，现都已刑满遣返香港；据悉，其患有哮喘，家属曾为其委托的大陆人权律师被强行辞退，转而让公派律师为其做有罪辩护；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其在香港的家属表示，最近两次给其寄信，都被狱方以无人领取而退回；又悉，其家属最后一次收到其信的日期是<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，后知其因哮喘而于同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-7</span>月被送进医院，至今其家人仍无法接收其信，且对其哮喘是否再次复发、狱中是否被罚和扣分、是否又被转换监等信息，均无所知。目前在广东省从化监狱（广东省广州市从化区鳌头镇聚丰北路<span lang="EN-US">623</span>号<span lang="EN-US">. </span>邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510940</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/3_11.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/3_11.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓静静<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，邓静静等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括邓静静在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。邓静静被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b
