lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯群豪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，汉族，初中毕业，住所地为广东省肇庆市四会市东城街道陶冲村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。冯群豪刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯瑞英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省建平县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生。家住辽宁省朝阳市建平县奎德素镇北山村六组。冯瑞英于一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮功。自中共一九九九年七月开始公开迫害法轮功后，冯瑞英遭到绑架、关押等多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在家中被建平县警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭建平县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。后被押入到马三家监狱迫害。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/27/2022-7-27.html#22726231132-10"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/27/2022-7-27.html#22726231132-10</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯少勇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯淑杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江鸡西虎林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1997</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，虎林市公安局国保大队刘强等多个警察在冯淑杰住宅的院落，将代亚军、冯淑杰夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕。之后又来了数个警察强行入室抄家，抢走了大法书籍、真相资料、电子产品等诸多私人物品。当天，冯淑杰被刑拘，送往鸡西市看守所关押，代亚军被关押在虎林市拘留所<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被密山法院开庭。冯淑杰被诬判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，代亚军被诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。冯淑杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b>信息来源</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E8%99%8E%E6%9E%97%E5%B8%82%E4%BB%A3%E4%BA%9A%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%86%AF%E6%B7%91%E6%9D%B0%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430324.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E8%99%8E%E6%9E%97%E5%B8%82%E4%BB%A3%E4%BA%9A%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%86%AF%E6%B7%91%E6%9D%B0%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430324.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯小妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏无锡市滨湖区拆迁受害者冯小妹，因被起诉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被无锡市滨湖区人民法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在无锡市第二看守所。冯小妹因房屋拆迁和家中财物被抢等问题，在当地始终无法解决，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日到北京天安门裸奔维权，被当地公安人员带回后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。在被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被无锡市公安局滨湖分局批准逮捕，在关押期间，冯小妹被两次强迫做精神病鉴定，其家人多次前往交涉无果，之后因为滨湖区雪浪街道要跟冯小妹谈拆迁问题，于是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日将她取保候审释放回家。在取保期间，冯小妹并未进京上访维权，却于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又被滨湖区法院以同样罪名批准逮捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭。后判决讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯颖军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京朝阳区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底，被海淀区清河派出所警察抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/26/446805.html#22725222336-9"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/26/446805.html#22725222336-9</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯勇军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，四川省绵阳市三台县人，原三台县百顷镇黄龙村二组<span lang="EN-US">023</span>号村民，现成都市金牛区金周路长住居民，实名举报人，人称“锦旗哥”，维权公民，中国在押维权人士。因冯勇军平素为人品行正直，凡其村中所遇不公之事均敢直言，以维护自己及村民的权益，故而颇得村民好评和认可，但却被村领导视为极好管闲事者而颇遭忌恨和报复性打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-11</span>日，曾因对村中外包养鱼的百顷水库被严重污染而不满，并就申请村里水库承包合同公开、水库资金流向等问题向当地政府提起多项行政诉讼以寻求救济而无果，而与<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位村民联合给三台县环保局和三台县百顷镇党委政府各送一面“不作为”锦旗，以示警示，遂被三台县警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘，并送三台县看守所关押；获释后，又因不服当地警方处罚决定，而曾实名举报三台县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日处置送“不作为”锦旗事件违法违规，以期公安部及四川省公安厅指令绵阳市警方调查处理，但结局却是绵阳市警方以情况汇报系工作秘密、国家机密、国家绝密为由而拒不告知；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因多次举报被警方非法限制人身自由和成都市青羊区警方行政不作为，并向青羊区法院提起诉讼，而被该法院以“属于刑事案件，不属于人民法院审查范围”为由作出多份行政裁定书，不予受理；后其被逼无奈，就多次持续报警并通过新浪微博声讨青羊区警方的不作为，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，遂被成都市青羊区警方以“扰乱单位秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因冯勇军第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>次来到四川高院蜀汉路办公区据悉投诉维权，而被成都市郫都区警方再次扣押，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被成都市郫都区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其已给其妻子亲笔留言要求帮请律师。目前被羁押于成都市新都区看守所（四川省成都市新都区鸿运大道西端<span lang="EN-US">800</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">610500</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_11.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_11.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯蕴青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丰晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毕业于山东师范大学新闻系，临沂市人大副调研员，副县级。二十多年公职期间因不满现有体制不被提拔，不允出国，不准考取研究生博士职称学历，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被市政府组织黑社会撞断腰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年春天退党退公职，单位拒绝。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月公开支持香港反送中，被送进派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠疫情间对体制内失察渎职，捐款贪污，罔顾人命，胡作非为忍无可忍，故上京发声。却被侮辱为精神病并强制治疗。丰晓燕拒不认罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被送至临沂第四精神病院，北京路育才路派出所二十多位警察，将患有腰椎间盘突出的丰晓燕在水泥地板拖行至住院部三楼，未进行精神检测，强行关进精神病医院。污蔑其为精神分裂症并强制用药。一直关押在精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，广东省深圳市人，“打工者中心劳动力”（<span lang="EN-US">Worker Empowerment</span>）工作人员，劳动法律咨询者，公益维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年始，其所在打工者中心以开展公益事业为己任，每年为至少<span lang="EN-US">500</span>名企业外来打工者提供免费法律咨询，举办超过<span lang="EN-US">200</span>余次免费文娱学习活动，使至少十万名工友受惠，因其亦参与其中，遂倍受基层工友的广泛欢迎；自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年以来，因焊接设备制造商深圳佳士科技<span lang="EN-US">(Jasic Technology)</span>与员工发生劳资冲突，佳士员工愤起维权抗议，其代表“打工者中心”前往调查介入，并与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名佳士工友积极尝试在中国大陆组建工会（类似于欧美国家里专门为工人谋福利的“工会”，而非“中华全国总工会”），遂遭到当局的严厉打击，被深圳警方多次传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，参与组建工会的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名工人因“试图成立非法工会”而被警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘押，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其因在警察局门外喊口号声援被抓工人，故而亦被深圳市坪山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”正式逮捕；据悉，其姐付红娥曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日为其递交“取保候审申请书”遭拒，理由是一旦批准申请，就“可能毁灭、伪造证据，干扰证人作证或者串供”，<span lang="EN-US">2019 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又在深圳市第二看守所给其汇款后被“查无此人”退回，迄今不予释放。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安丰盛基督教教会教徒。自从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日西安市十里铺派出所以“诈骗罪”为由将西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师带走，现已被执行指定居所监视居住，另外一位教会的同工廉旭亮，也以同一罪名被执行指定居所监视居住。还有一位教会会友付娟也被密押一直未放，罪名尚不明悉。目前三人均被关押在政府指定的某个地方。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付瑞英<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日判付瑞英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">傅胜平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">深圳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖南省岳阳人，居住在深圳市龙岗区坂田街道荔园新村小区。因为讲述法轮功被迫害真相，她分别于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，两次被龙岗区公安分局警察拘禁，各<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被龙岗公安分局警察抓捕。后得知，她于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，已被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/22/447953.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/22/447953.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b 0pt;">付淑贤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨平房区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，付淑贤被开庭时不让与家人见面，已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现身体状况不正常，不能行走。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436376.html#2212231914-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436376.html#2212231914-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">傅炫娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，汉族，中专学历，原籍地是广西壮族自治区北海市合浦县常乐镇大教村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付燕飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">长春法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，毕业于东北师范大学生命科学学院本科，是高中教师，于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年毕业前夕开始修炼法轮功，因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚，付燕飞因在劳动公园讲真相，被受中共谎言毒害的人诬告，后被和顺街派出所抓捕，被朝阳区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，付燕飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
